(the view expressed in) the s┼лtra (is that) of Aupamanyav─лputra. Baudh─Бyana indeed says here that for those who count nine Vihavya rks, one should add fuel to the fires with the Vihavya verses-each one with three verses. For those who count eight, one should repeat the first or the last one. For those who count ten, one should add fuel to each one with three verses, and should recite the tenth standing to the north of the ─Аhavan─лya, ┼Ъ─Бl─лki indeed says here that fuel is added to the G─Бrhapatya once.

English

The Anv─Бh─Бryapacana fire is procured from a secular source. One should therefore add fuel only to the ─Аhavan─лya fire with a Vihavya verse; and should recite the remaining verses while standing towards the north of the ─Аhavan─лya. Aupamanyava says that one should add fuel to the fires with Vihavya verses to each one with a verse; and recite the remaining verses while standing to the north of the ─Аhavan─лya. Maudgalya says that one should add fuel only to the ─Аhavan─лya with the verses, “I receive Agni who ascends a good chariot, who grants happiness and who appears following the rising sun by day, the ─Аditya the highest luminary among the luminaries. May he remain for the offering to deities.

Aupamanyava holds the view (similar to that of ┼Ъ─Бl─лki) and further adds that hereafter the Agnip─Бvam─Бni verses should be employed neither for the ─Аhavan─лya nor for G─Бrhapatya; they may be employed merely for scriptural study.
